access / ˈækses /
n. 入口，通道；获得的机会，使用权；（对计算机存储器的）访问，存取；（情感）爆发，发作；探视权
v. 接近，进入；获取，访问（计算机信息）
adj. <美>（电视节目或时间等）对外公开的
[例]
1.Does the hotel have wheelchair access ?这家旅馆有轮椅通道吗？。
2.She had unhindered access to the files. 她可任意使用档案。
3.There is no vehicular access. 不通车。
[搭]
1.random access 随机存取；随机访问；随机接入；随机读取
2.Access Control 访问控制；存取控制；权限控制；门禁控制
3.direct memory access 直接存储器访问；直接存储器存取；直接内存存取；直接记忆体存取
4.access control 访问控制
5.have access to 使用；接近；可以利用
6.internet access 互联网接入
[联]a + cess ——> 一 + 进入，接近 ——> 可以通过某种方式进入或使用的东西

accessibility / əkˌsesəˈbɪləti /
n.（地方）易于进入性，（物品）易于接近性；易使用性，可及性；易懂性
[例]
1.In other words, Voltaire's amateurism in science "was a source of his contemporary appeal, demonstrating for the first time the accessibility of Newton's ideas to nonspecialists". 换句话说，伏尔泰在科学上的业余性“是他当时吸引力的一个来源，第一次证明了牛顿的思想对非专业人士的可接受性”。
2.Seminar topics are chosen for their accessibility to a general audience. 专题讨论会的话题是根据普通听众的理解力来选定的。
3.Pay attention to accessibility. 注意一下可访问性。
[搭]
1.Web Accessibility 网页易操作设计；网络无障碍；无障碍网路空间
2.Accessibility Options 辅助功能选项；辅助选项；单击辅助选项按钮；帮助功效选项
3.service accessibility 服务可得到性；业务接入；业务接入性
[联]ac (一再) + cess (行走) + ibility (形容词后缀) ——> 一再行走的能力

accessible / əkˈsesəb(ə)l /
adj. 可到达的，可进入的；易得到的，可使用的；可以理解的，易懂的；平易近人的，随和的；易受影响的
[例]
1.The centre is easily accessible to the general public. 该中心对于广大公众来讲很便利。
2.The museum is easily accessible by car. 开车可以方便地到达博物馆。
3.These documents are not accessible to the public. 公众无法看到这些文件。
[搭]
1.accessible roof 可到达的屋顶；有通道的屋顶；可达到的屋顶
2.accessible point 数  可达点；接触点
3.accessible surface 可及表面
4.readily accessible 易接近的；易达到的；可存取的
[联]ac + cess + ible ——> 能接近的，可进入的

accessories / əkˈsesəriz /
n. 附件（accessory 的复数形式）；辅助程序
[例]
1.The first catalogue featured speciality shavers, accessories, and cutlery. 第一份目录主要介绍专业剃须刀、配件和刀具。
2.One such partnership is with Elvis&Kresse, an accessories brand working with reclaimed materials. 其中一个合作伙伴是 Elvis&Kresse，一个使用再生材料的配件品牌。
3.Some people bring along a lot of accessories like extra lenses, but there's really no need for this class. 有些人会带很多配件，比如额外的镜片，但对于这门课来说真的没有必要。
[搭]
1.bathroom accessories 浴室配件；卫浴配件；浴室组成一套装配
2.Hair Accessories 发饰；头饰；发饰品；假发配件
3.apparel and accessories 服饰；衣饰；装饰品；装饰人体的物品总称
4.fashion accessories 时尚饰品；流行配件
5.motorcycle accessories 摩托车配件
[联]ac (到达) + cess (行走) + ories (复数形式，表示类别或状态) ——> 可以到达行走类别或状态

accessory / əkˈsesəri /
n. 附件，配件；装饰品，配饰；同谋，从犯
adj. 辅助的，副的；附属的；同谋的
[例]
1.He was charged with being an accessory to murder. 他被控为谋杀罪的从犯。
2.The company serves the national automotive aftermarket with a broad range of accessory and recreational-vehicle products. 该公司为全国机动车售后市场提供各种配件和休闲车产品。
3.For this reason, the watch industry has become an accessory business in recent years. 正因如此，手表行业近年来已成为配件行业。
[搭]
1.accessory nerve 副神经；胸锁乳突肌
2.accessory fruit 附果；假果；副果
3.accessory pigment 辅助色素；辅色素
4.accessory equipment 辅助设备
6.accessory ingredient 助剂；配合剂
[联]ac (尖端) + cess (行走) + ory (场所) ——> 存放尖端行走工具的场所

accredit / əˈkredɪt /
v. 把……归于，归因于；委派；信任，正式认可；授权
[例]
1.They accredit these views to him. 他们认定这些是他的见解。
2.We accredit him with finding that book. 我们相信是他找到那本书的。
3.vt.  We accredit the invention of the electric light to Adison. 我们把电灯的发明归功于爱迪生。
[搭]
1.Install and Accredit Systems 对系统实施安装和授权
2.accredit ation 委派
3.endow with accredit 赋能授权
[联]accredit (授权) + ate (动词后缀) ——> 授予权力

accreditation / əˌkredɪˈteɪʃ(ə)n /
n. 委派；信赖；鉴定合格
[例]
1.The university's law school failed to win full accreditation from the American Bar Association. 这所大学的法学院没能获得美国律师协会的完整认可。
2.The American Telemedicine Association and other organizations have started accreditation programs to identify top-quality telemedicine sites. 美国远程医疗协会等组织已经发起认证程序用以识别最优质的远程医疗网站。
3.Check to see if accreditation is in its future. 检查确认一下该校将来是否会被官方认可。
[搭]
1.International Accreditation Forum 国际认可论坛；国际认证论坛；国际授权论坛
2.accreditation body 认可机构；认证机构；审定团体；巴西的国家认可机构
3.accreditation system 认可体系；制证系统；认证制度
[联]accredit (授权) + ation (名词后缀) ——> 认证，官方许可

accusation / ˌækjuˈzeɪʃ(ə)n /
n. 控告，指责，谴责；（尚未证实的被控告的）罪名，罪状
[例]
1.She was deeply pained by the accusation. 这一指控使她极为痛苦。
2.He took the ridiculous accusation in stride. 他从容应对那荒谬的指控。
3.There was a hint of accusation in her voice. 她的话音中暗含谴责的意思。
[搭]
1.accusation function 控诉职能
2.agency for accusation 代理控告；代理控诉
3.accusation letter box 检举箱
[联]accu (精确地) + sation (状态) ——> 指控的状态，即指控

accuse / əˈkjuːz /
v. 控告，指控；指责，谴责，归咎于
[例]
1.He laughs loudly when I accuse him of fibbing. 我指控他撒谎时，他笑得很大声。
2.His father would accuse him of neglecting his filial duties. 他父亲会指控他没有尽孝。
3.Politicians accuse the media of talking up the possibility of a riot. 政客们谴责媒体夸大骚乱的可能性。
[搭]
1.accuse of 因某事控告某人；指控
2.accuse sb of doing sth 指控某人做某事
3.accuse sb of 指责；指责某人干某事；指控；指责某人
[联]accuse (指责，控告) + se (后缀，表示动作) ——> 指责

accuser / əˈkjuːzə(r) /
n. 原告；控告者；指责者
[例]
1.None remained but the two officials, the accused, the accuser, and Miles Hendon. 除了两名官员、被告、原告和迈尔斯·亨顿外，没有人留下。
2.Everyone will know who the accuser is. 所有人都会知道原告是谁。
3.But the accuser kept changing her story. 但原告一直在变换她的故事。
[搭]
1.ronan the accuser 指控者·罗南；指控者罗南；李培斯
2.attack accuser 反击对手；攻击原告；反击指控者
3.attack the accuser 攻击指控者
[联]accuser (控告者) + accuse (控告) ——> 提出指控的人

accustom / əˈkʌstəm /
v. 使习惯于，使适应于
[例]
1.She tried to accustom herself to the tight bandages. 她尝试着使自己习惯那些紧绷的绷带。

3.When one has been in a family circle one cannot accustom oneself to this life!当一个人已经在家庭圈子里，他无法习惯于这种生活！。
[搭]
1.accustom oneself 习惯于
2.accustom custom 习惯风俗
[联]ac + custom ——> 习惯于

agree / əˈɡriː /
v. 同意，赞成；答应，接受；达成一致意见；商定，约定；相符，吻合；赞同；（语法）呼应；批准，认可（计划、要求等）；适合（某人）
[例]
1.I don't agree with spanking. 我不赞成打屁股。
2.I'm half inclined to agree. 我不十分同意。
3.I entirely agree with you. 我完全同意你的看法。
[搭]
1.agree with 适合；同意某人；符合
2.agree in 在…方面意见一致；在…相同
3.agree to do sth 同意做某事；同意干某事；赞成做某事；批准做某事
4.agree on 对…取得一致意见
[联]a +gree (同意) ——> 同意

3.agreeable to taste 味鲜可口
[联]ag + ree + able ——> 同意的 + 能够 + 可以的 → 表示令人愉快的、合意的

2.According to a recent survey, most children feel disgusted if their parents stalk or follow their accounts anonymously on social media. 根据最近的一项调查，大多数孩子对父母在社交媒体上匿名跟踪或关注他们的账户感到厌恶。

appeal / əˈpiːl /
n. 呼吁，恳求；上诉，申诉；吸引力，感染力；（为慈善或正义事业的）募捐；启发，打动

2.We must broaden our appeal. 我们必须扩大我们的吸引力。
3.My appeal proved futile. 我的呼吁白费了。
[搭]
1.appeal to 呼吁；吸引；要求；诉诸
2.Court of Appeal 法  上诉法院；上诉庭；中级法院
3.appeal to fear 诉诸恐惧
4.appeal for 恳求，请求；要求
5.sex appeal 性感；吸引力
6.appeal against 提出上诉
[联]appeal (恳求，上诉) + ear (耳朵) ——> 向耳朵恳求

appear / əˈpɪr /
v. 出现，呈现；首次使用，起源；出庭；演出，出场；出版，发表；记载，提及；看来，似乎；表现得……；<非正式>到达
[例]
1.She will appear in court tomorrow. 她明天出庭。
2.At dusk bats appear in vast numbers. 蝙蝠于傍晚时分大批出现。
3.Cracks began to appear in the walls. 墙壁开始出现裂缝了。

5.appear on 在. . . 上出现

[联]a + ppear ——> 到达 + （表面）——> 显现

appearance / əˈpɪrəns /
n. 露面，演出；出庭，到场；外表，外观；表面现象，假象；出现；起源，问世；表现；出版，广播

1.Journalists were given the freedom to visit, investigate, and report without constraint. 新闻记者被赋予在没有约束下参观、调查和报道的自由。
2.The boy felt constraint in her presence. 那男孩在她面前感到局促不安。
3.The terrible constraint on organ transplantation is that every life extended depends on the death of someone young enough and healthy enough to have organs worth transplanting. 器官移植的可怕约束是，一个人生命的延长要依赖于另一个足够年轻、健康的人的死亡，因为只有这些人身上才有值得移植的器官。
[搭]
1.budget constraint 预算线；预算约束；预算限制；预算约束线
2.Link Constraint 链接约束；连接约束；连结约束；链接限制
3.Constraint programming 限制规划；限制程序设计
4.constraint condition 约束条件
5.constraint equation 约束方程式
6.budget constraint 预算约束；预算限制
[联]con (一起) + strain (拉紧) ——> 约束

enactive / ɪˈnæktɪv /
adj. 法律制定的；有制定权的
[例]
1.EnactiveEnactivism argues that cognition arises through a dynamic interaction between an acting organism and its environment.  It claims that our environment is one which we selectively create through our capacities to interact with the world.  "Organisms do not passively receive information from their environments, which they then translate into internal representations.  Natural cognitive systems. . . participate in the generation of meaning . . . engaging in transformational and not merely informational interactions: they enact a world. " These authors suggest that the increasing emphasis upon enactive terminology presages a new era in thinking about cognitive science.  How the actions involved in enactivism relate to age-old questions about free will remains a topic of active debate. The term 'enactivism' is close in meaning to 'enaction', defined as "the manner in which a subject of perception creatively matches its actions to the requirements of its situation".  The introduction of the term enaction in this context is attributed to Francisco Varela, Evan Thompson, and Eleanor Rosch, who proposed the name to "emphasize the growing conviction that cognition is not the representation of a pre-given world by a pre-given mind but is rather the enactment of a world and a mind on the basis of a history of the variety of actions that a being in the world performs".  This was further developed by Thompson and others, to place emphasis upon the idea that experience of the world is a result of mutual interaction between the sensorimotor capacities of the organism and its environment. The initial emphasis of enactivism upon sensorimotor skills has been criticized as "cognitively marginal", but it has been extended to apply to higher level cognitive activities, such as social interactions.  "In the enactive view,. . .  knowledge is constructed: it is constructed by an agent through its sensorimotor interactions with its environment, co-constructed between and within living species through their meaningful interaction with each other.  In its most abstract form, knowledge is co-constructed between human individuals in socio-linguistic interactions. . . Science is a particular form of social knowledge construction. . . [that] allows us to perceive and predict events beyond our immediate cognitive grasp. . . and also to construct further, even more powerful scientific knowledge. "Enactivism is closely related to situated cognition and embodied cognition, and is presented as an alternative to cognitivism, computationalism and Cartesian dualism. 。
[搭]
1.enactive representation 动作表征；动作表象；动作性表征
2.enactive representation stage 动作表象阶段
3.Enactive cognition 生成认知
[联]enactive (有作用的，实施的) + act (行动，行为) ——> 有作用的行为

3.Her introduction is a model of fairness, a lively summation of Irish history. 她的导论是公正的典范，是对爱尔兰历史的总结。
[搭]
1.Justice as Fairness 作为公平的正义；公平的正义；正义即公平

3.Marketplace Fairness Act 市场公平法案；市场公平法
4.judicial fairness 司法公正
[联]fairness (公平) + ness (名词后缀) ——> 公平性

normative / ˈnɔːmətɪv /

[例]
1.The sentence defines normative ethics by specifying the sense of the "norms" for which it searches. 这个句子通过指定它所寻找的“规范”的意义来定义规范性伦理。
2.In searching for norms in the sense of authoritative standards of what ought to be, rather than in the sense of what is average and thus can be considered normal, normative ethics aims to dictate. 在寻求规范的过程中，就意义上而言，寻找的是规定的权威标准规范，而不是从平均的角度被认定为常态化，规范的伦理目的在于指示。
3.The method is relatively normative and notional and structurely. 该方法是概念上和结构上相对规范。
[搭]
1.normative economics 经  规范经济学；规范分析；规范

penalty / ˈpenəlti /

proto / ˈprəʊtəʊ /

3.Proto-Indo-European is a reconstructed language, meaning, it is what linguists concluded a parent language of Sanskrit, Latin and Greek would have to be like. 原始印欧语是一门经过重构得出的语言，也就是说，这就是语言学家总结出梵语、拉丁语和希腊语的母系语言的样子。

protocol / ˈprəʊtəkɒl /
n. 礼仪，礼节；国际议定书，协议；条约草案，（协议或条约的）附件；（协定，公约）修正案（或增补）；（数据传递的）协议，规约；科学实验计划，医疗方案；（科学实验结果的）官方记录
v. 以协议形式发布；拟定
[例]
1.While SIP is a request-response protocol, there is not necessarily only one response to every one request. 虽然 SIP 是请求-响应协议，但每个请求不一定只有一个响应与之对应。
2.Cerf has been working with NASA's Pasadena Jet Propulsion Laboratory—the people behind the recent Mars expedition—to design what he calls an "interplanetary Internet protocol. "瑟夫一直在与美国宇航局的帕萨迪纳喷气推进实验室（最近火星探测的幕后人员）合作，设计他所说的“星际互联网协议”。
3.The Kyoto Protocol, which set different duties for all countries to cut emissions, states that different countries should reduce their collective greenhouse emissions accordingly. 《京都议定书》为各国设定了不同的减排义务，规定各国应相应地减少各自的温室气体排放总量。
[搭]
1.Montreal Protocol 蒙特利尔协议；蒙特利尔协定
2.Kyoto Protocol 京都议定书；京都协定
3.routing protocol 路由协议；路由选择协议；路由协定；路由选择和谈
4.communication protocol[计]通信协议
5.kyoto protocol 京都议定书
6.network protocol 网络协议
[联]pro (向前) + tocol (规则) ——> 前进的规则

proton / ˈproʊtɑːn /
n. [物]质子
n.（Proton）人名；（法）普罗东
[例]
1.Every time you had one more proton, you had another element. 每发现多一个质子，就会多一种元素。
2.Only then can they hope to describe conditions at the Big Bang, when all space and time was compressed into a volume far smaller than a proton. 只有那样他们才能指望描述大爆炸的情况，所有的空间和时间全部在那时被压缩成一个远小于质子的体积。
3.Heavy water is heavy because the hydrogen in it weighs twice as much as ordinary hydrogen (it has a proton and a neutron in its nucleus, instead of just a proton). 重水之所以重是因为水中氢的重量是普通氢的两倍（它的原子核中有一个质子和一个中子，而不仅仅是一个质子）。

[联]re + strict + ive ——> 再严格一点的，带有约束性的

3.Due to the restrictively narrow site in an area between the city centre and its eastern suburbs, the tower is arranged as a cluster of three parallel elongated blocks. 由于在城市中心和其东侧城郊间的相当狭窄的基地，建筑被布置为三个平行的细长块群。

[联]re + strict + ive ——> 重新严格地做某事

3.I'm surprised you fell for that trick. 我感到惊奇，你竟中了那个诡计。
[搭]
1.hat-trick 帽子戏法；球中指连续使三个击球员退场；同一人连进三球
2.do the trick 达到理想的结果；做成功；做胜利；到达幻想的成果
3.trick or treat 不招待就使坏（指万圣节孩子们挨家逐户要糖果等礼物，如不遂愿便恶作剧一番的风俗）
4.do the trick 获得成功
[联]deceive (欺骗) + craft (技巧，手艺) ——> 欺骗的技巧

trickle / ˈtrɪkl /
v.（使）滴，淌；（小批地）慢慢移动；（球）缓慢滚动
n. 慢速移动；滴，淌，细流
[例]
1.There was not so much as a trickle of water. 一点儿细流的水也没有。

3.The stream has thinned down to a mere trickle. 这条小河变成细流了。
[搭]
1.trickle irrigation 农工  滴灌；滴灌系统；冲洗法

3.Trickle-down Effect 涓滴效应；滴流效应；滴漏效应
4.trickle down 向下滴流
[联]trickle (细流，滴流) + leak (泄漏) ——> 细微的泄漏

withdraw / wɪðˈdrɔː /
v. 提，取（银行账户中的钱款）；停止提供，不再给予； 退出，不参加；（军队）撤离； 脱离（社会），不与人交往；离开；（将某物从某地或位置）抽回，移开；撤回，收回（前言）；（从某物中）拿出；停止提供，召回；退出，返回（至另一个房间）；（因对工作时间、报酬等不满意而）罢工；取消（许可、邀请或提议）；戒毒
[例]

2.There have been calls for Britain to withdraw from the EU. 一直有人呼吁英国退出欧盟。
3.He refused to withdraw derogatory remarks made about his boss. 他拒绝收回对自己老板的贬抑之言。
[搭]
1.to withdraw an offer 撤回报盘；撤消报盘；撤销报盘；撤报答盘
2.withdraw cash 取钱；提取现金；取现；取现金
3.withdraw money 取钱；提款；提钱；取回存款
4.withdraw from 退出；离开
[联]with (带有）+ draw (拉回）——> 撤回

[联]with (带有) + draw (拉，取) + al (形容词后缀) ——> 撤回，撤退

withstood / wɪðˈstʊd /

5.voltage withstand 耐电压
